 320→\n   321→    private void buildAndVerifyTopology(final InternalTopologyBuilder builder) {\n   322→        builder.rewriteTopology(config);\n   323→        builder.buildTopology();\n   324→\n   325→        final Set<String> allInputTopicsCopy = new HashSet<>(allInputTopics);\n   326→\n   327→        // As we go, check each topology for overlap in the set of input topics/patterns\n   328→        final int numInputTopics = allInputTopicsCopy.size();\n   329→        final List<String> inputTopics = builder.fullSourceTopicNames();\n   330→        final Collection<String> inputPatterns = numNewInputTopics) {\n   339→            inputTopics.retainAll(allInputTopicsCopy);\n   340→            inputPatterns.retainAll(allInputTopicsCopy);\n   341→            log.error(\"Tried to add the TopologyException(\"Named Topologies may not subscribe to the same input topics or patterns\");\n   344→        }\n   345→\n   346→        final ProcessorTopology globalTopology = public int numStreamThreads(final StreamsConfig config) {\n   361→        final int configuredNumStreamThreads = config.getInt(StreamsConfig.NUM_STREAM_THREADS_CONFIG);\n   362→\n   363→        // If version.topologyLock.lock();\n            final long latestTopologyVersion = topologyVersion();\n            handleTopologyAdditions.accept(namedTopologiesView());\n            handleTopologyRemovals.accept(namedTopologiesView());\n            threadVersions.put(Thread.currentThread().getName(), latestTopologyVersion);\n        } finally {\n            version.topologyLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void maybeNotifyTopologyVersionListeners() {\n        try {\n            lock();\n            final long minThreadVersion = minimumThreadVersion();\n            final Iterator<TopologyVersionListener> iterator = version.activeTopologyUpdateListeners.listIterator();\n            TopologyVersionListener topologyVersionListener;\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                topologyVersionListener = iterator.next();\n                final long topologyVersionWaitersVersion = topologyVersionListener.topologyVersion;\n                if (minThreadVersion >= topologyVersionWaitersVersion) {\n                    topologyVersionListener.future.complete(null);\n                    iterator.remove();\n                    log.info(\"All threads are now on topology version {}\", topologyVersionListener.topologyVersion);\n                }\n            }\n        } finally {\n            unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Return the minimum version across all live threads, or Long.MAX_VALUE if there are no threads running\n    private long minimumThreadVersion() {\n        final Optional<Long> minVersion = threadVersions.values().stream().min(Long::compare);\n        return minVersion.orElse(Long.MAX_VALUE);\n    }\n\n    public void wakeupThreads() {\n        try {\n            lock();\n            version.topologyCV.signalAll();\n        } finally {\n            unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void maybeWaitForNonEmptyTopology(final Supplier<StreamThread.State> threadState) {\n        if (isEmpty() && threadState.get().isAlive()) {\n            try {\n                lock();\n                while (isEmpty() && threadState.get().isAlive()) {\n                    try {\n                        log.debug(\"Detected that the topology is currently empty, waiting for something to process\");\n                        version.topologyCV.await();\n                    } catch (final InterruptedException e) {\n                        log.error(\"StreamThread was interrupted while waiting on empty topology\", e);\n                    }\n                }\n            } finally {\n                unlock();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Adds the topology and registers a future that listens for all threads on the older version to see the update\n     */\n    public void registerAndBuildNewTopology(final KafkaFutureImpl<Void> future, final InternalTopologyBuilder newTopologyBuilder) {\n newTopologyBuilder.topologyName(), version.topologyVersion.get());\n            version.topologyVersion.incrementAndGet();\n            version.activeTopologyUpdateListeners.add(new            result.complete(null);\n   194→            return result;\n   195→        }\n   196→\n   197→        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n   198→            lockedTasks.addAll(taskIds);\n );\n   248→    }\n   249→\n   250→    @Override\n   251→    public void unlockTasks(final Set<TaskId> taskIds) {\n   252→\n   253→        if (taskIds.isEmpty()) {\n   254→            return;\n   255→ It's assigned to one of the executors for processing.\n * 2. It's locked for committing, removal, other manipulations etc.\n * 3. Neither 1 or 2, i.e. it stays idle. This is possible if we do not have enough executors or because those tasks\n *    are not processable (e.g. because no records fetched) yet.\n */\npublic final class DefaultTaskManager implements TaskManager {\n\n    private final Time time;\n    private final Logger log;\n    private final TasksRegistry tasks;\n\n    private final Lock tasksLock = new ReentrantLock();\n    private final Condition tasksCondition = tasksLock.newCondition();\n    private final List<TaskId> lockedTasks = new ArrayList<>();\n    private final Map<TaskId, StreamsException> uncaughtExceptions = new HashMap<>();\n    private final Map<TaskId, TaskExecutor> assignedTasks = new HashMap<>();\n    private final TaskExecutionMetadata taskExecutionMetadata;\n\n    private final List<TaskExecutor> taskExecutors;\n\n    public static class DefaultTaskExecutorCreator implements TaskExecutorCreator {\n        @Override\n        public TaskExecutor create(final TaskManager taskManager, final String name, final Time time, final TaskExecutionMetadata taskExecutionMetadata) {\n            return new DefaultTaskExecutor(taskManager, name, time, taskExecutionMetadata);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public DefaultTaskManager(final Time time,\n                              final String clientId,\n                              final TasksRegistry tasks,\n                              final TaskExecutorCreator executorCreator,\n                              final TaskExecutionMetadata taskExecutionMetadata,\n                              final int numExecutors\n                              ) {\n        final String logPrefix = String.format(\"%s \", clientId);\n        final LogContext logContext = new LogContext(logPrefix);\n        this.log = logContext.logger(DefaultTaskManager.class);\n        this.time = time;\n        this.tasks = tasks;\n        this.taskExecutionMetadata = taskExecutionMetadata;\n\n        this.taskExecutors = new ArrayList<>(numExecutors);\n        for (int i = 1; i <= numExecutors; i++) {\n            final String name = clientId + \"-TaskExecutor-\" + i;\n            this.taskExecutors.add(executorCreator.create(this, name, time, taskExecutionMetadata));\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public StreamTask assignNextTask(final TaskExecutor executor) {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            if (!taskExecutors.contains(executor)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The requested executor for getting next task to assign is unrecognized\");\n            }\n\n            // the most naive scheduling algorithm for now: give the next unlocked, unassigned, and  processable task\n            for (final StreamTask task : tasks.activeInitializedTasks()) {\n                if (!assignedTasks.containsKey(task.id()) &&\n                    !lockedTasks.contains(task.id()) &&\n                    canProgress(task, time.milliseconds()) &&\n                    !hasUncaughtException(task.id())\n                ) {\n\n                    assignedTasks.put(task.id(), executor);\n\n                    log.debug(\"Assigned task {} to executor {}\", task.id(), executor.name());\n\n                    return task;\n                }\n            }\n\n            log.debug(\"Found no assignable task InterruptedException {\n        final boolean interrupted = returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            for (final StreamTask task : tasks.activeInitializedTasks()) {\n                if (!assignedTasks.containsKey(task.id()) &&\n                    !lockedTasks.contains(task.id()) &&\n                    canProgress(task, time.milliseconds()) &&\n                    !hasUncaughtException(task.id())\n                ) {\n                    log.debug(\"Await unblocked: returning early from await since a processable task {} was found\", task.id());\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n            try {\n                // We re-check the shutdownRequest atomic boolean to avoid a race condition. If this thread was\n                // previously interrupted while awaiting tasksCondition, it is possible to miss the signalAll that\n                // is called during shutdown. If this happens, we end up blocking in the await forever.\n                if (!isShuttingDown.get()) {\n                    log.debug(\"Await blocking\");\n                    tasksCondition.await();\n                } else {\n                    log.debug(\"Not awaiting since shutdown was requested\");\n                }\n            } catch (final InterruptedException ignored) {\n                // we interrupt the thread for shut down and pause.\n                // we can ignore this exception.\n                log.debug(\"Await unblocked: Interrupted while waiting for processable tasks\");\n                return true;\n            }\n            log.debug(\"Await unblocked: Woken up to check for processable tasks\");\n            return false;\n        });\n\n        if (interrupted) {\n            throw new InterruptedException();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void signalTaskExecutors() {\n        log.debug(\"Waking up task executors\");\n        executeWithTasksLocked(tasksCondition::signalAll);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void unassignTask(final StreamTask task, final TaskExecutor executor) {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            if (!taskExecutors.contains(executor)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The requested executor for unassign task is unrecognized\");\n            }\n\n            final TaskExecutor lockedExecutor = assignedTasks.get(task.id());\n            if (lockedExecutor == null || lockedExecutor != executor) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Task \" + task.id() + \" is not locked by the executor\");\n            }\n\n            assignedTasks.remove(task.id());\n\n            log.debug(\"Unassigned {} from executor {}\", task.id(), executor.name());\n            tasksCondition.signalAll();\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public KafkaFuture<Void> lockTasks(final Set<TaskId> taskIds) {\n        final KafkaFutureImpl<Void> result = new KafkaFutureImpl<>();\n\n        if (taskIds.isEmpty()) {\n            result.complete(null);\n            return result;\n        }\n\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            lockedTasks.addAll(taskIds);\n\n            final Set<TaskId> remainingTaskIds = new ConcurrentSkipListSet<>(taskIds);\n\n            for (final TaskId taskId : taskIds) {\n                final Task task = tasks.initializedTask(taskId);\n\n                if (task == null) {\n                    throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Trying to lock task \" + taskId + \" but it's not owned\");\n                }\n\n                if (!task.isActive()) {\n                    throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The locking task \" + taskId + \" is not an active task\");\n                }\n\n                if (assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                    final TaskExecutor executor = assignedTasks.get(taskId);\n                    log.debug(\"Requesting release of task {} from {}\", taskId, executor.name());\n                    final KafkaFuture<StreamTask> future = executor.unassign();\n                    future.whenComplete((streamTask, throwable) -> {\n                        if (throwable != null) {\n                            result.completeExceptionally(throwable);\n                        } else {\n                            assert !assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId);\n                            // It can happen that the executor handed back the task before we asked it to\n                            // in which case `streamTask` will be null here.\n                            assert streamTask == null || streamTask.id() == taskId;\n                            remainingTaskIds.remove(taskId);\n                            if (remainingTaskIds.isEmpty()) {\n                                result.complete(null);\n                            }\n                        }\n                    });\n                } else {\n                    remainingTaskIds.remove(taskId);\n                    if (remainingTaskIds.isEmpty()) {\n                        result.complete(null);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            return result;\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public KafkaFuture<Void> lockAllTasks() {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() ->\n            lockTasks(tasks.activeInitializedTasks().stream().map(Task::id).collect(Collectors.toSet()))\n        );\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void         log.debug(\"Waking up task executors\");\n            tasksCondition.signalAll();\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void unlockAllTasks() {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> still assigned to executors\");\n            }\n\n            if (!lockedTasks.contains(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The task to remove is not locked yet by the task manager\");\n            }\n\n            if (!tasks.containsInitialized(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The task to remove is not owned by the task manager\");\n            }\n\n            tasks.removeTask(tasks.initializedTask(taskId));\n        });\n\n        log.info(\"Removed task {} from the task manager\", taskId);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Set<ReadOnlyTask> getTasks() {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> tasks.activeInitializedTasks().stream().map(ReadOnlyTask::new).collect(Collectors.toSet()));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setUncaughtException(final StreamsException exception, final TaskId taskId) {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n\n            if (!assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"An uncaught exception can only be set as long as the task is still assigned\");\n            }\n\n            if (uncaughtExceptions.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The uncaught exception must be cleared before restarting processing\");\n            }\n\n            uncaughtExceptions.put(taskId, exception);\n        });\n\n        log.info(\"Set an uncaught exception of type {} for task {}, with error message: {}\",\n            exception.getClass().getName(),\n            taskId,\n            exception.getMessage());\n    }\n\n    public Map<TaskId, RuntimeException> drainUncaughtExceptions() {\n        final Map<TaskId, RuntimeException> returnValue = returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            final Map<TaskId, RuntimeException> result = new HashMap<>(uncaughtExceptions);\n            uncaughtExceptions.clear();\n            return result;\n        });\n\n        if (!returnValue.isEmpty()) {\n            log.debug(\"Drained {} uncaught exceptions\", returnValue.size());\n        }\n\n        return returnValue;\n    }\n\n    public boolean hasUncaughtException(final TaskId taskId) {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> uncaughtExceptions.containsKey(taskId));\n    }\n\n    private void executeWithTasksLocked(final Runnable action) {\n        tasksLock.lock();\n        try {\n            action.run();\n        } finally {\n            tasksLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private <T> T returnWithTasksLocked(final Supplier<T> action) {\n        tasksLock.lock();\n        try {\n            return action.get();\n        } finally {\n            tasksLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private boolean canProgress(final StreamTask task, final long nowMs) {\n        return\n            taskExecutionMetadata.canProcessTask(task, nowMs) && task.isProcessable(nowMs) ||\n                taskExecutionMetadata.canPunctuateTask(task) && (task.canPunctuateStreamTime() || task.canPunctuateSystemTime());\n    }\n\n    public void startTaskExecutors() {\n        for (final TaskExecutor t: during rebalancing\n * the shard may change, which triggers listener notifications.\n */\npublic class MetricsSessionManager {\n\n    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(MetricsSessionManager.class);\n\n    private final ReentrantLock sessionLock = new ReentrantLock();\n    private final Condition sessionReady = sessionLock.newCondition();\n    private final long sessionTtlMs;\n\n    private volatile MetricsSession currentSession;\n    private boolean rebalancingMode = false;\n\n    private final List<MetricsSessionListener> listeners = new CopyOnWriteArrayList<>();\n\n    public MetricsSessionManager(final long sessionTtlMs) {\n        this.sessionTtlMs = sessionTtlMs;\n        this.currentSession = new MetricsSession(\n            \"init-\" + ThreadLocalRandom.current().nextInt(10000),\n            0,\n            System.currentTimeMillis() + sessionTtlMs\n        );\n    }\n\n    public void registerListener(final MetricsSessionListener listener) {\n        listeners.add(listener);\n    }\n\n    public void setRebalancingMode(final boolean rebalancing) {\n        sessionLock.lock();\n        try {\n            this.rebalancingMode = rebalancing;\n            log.debug(\"Metrics session manager rebalancing mode set to {}\", rebalancing);\n        } finally {\n            sessionLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns the current session. The returned reference is safe to read\n     * without holding the lock due to the volatile field, but the session\n     * may expire at any time.\n     */\n    public MetricsSession currentSession() {\n        return currentSession;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * If the current session has expired, renew it.\n     */\n    public void refreshSessionIfExpired() {\n        sessionLock.lock();\n        try {\n            if (currentSession != null && currentSession.expiryMs > System.currentTimeMillis()) {\n                return; // still valid\n            }\n            renewSessionInternal();\n        } finally {\n            sessionLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Force a session renewal regardless of expiry status.\n     */\n    public void renewSession() {\n        sessionLock.lock();\n        try {\n            renewSessionInternal();\n        } finally {\n            sessionLock.unlock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private void renewSessionInternal() {\n        final MetricsSession oldSession = currentSession;\n        final int newShardId;\n        if (rebalancingMode) {\n            // During rebalancing, the shard assignment may change\n            newShardId = ThreadLocalRandom.current().nextInt(1024);\n        } else {\n            newShardId = oldSession != null ? oldSession.shardId : 0;\n        }\n\n        final MetricsSession newSession = new MetricsSession(\n            \"sess-\" + ThreadLocalRandom.current().nextInt(100000),\n            newShardId,\n            System.currentTimeMillis() + sessionTtlMs\n        );\n        currentSession = newSession;\n        log.debug(\"Renewed metrics session: old={}, new={}\", oldSession, newSession);\n\n        notifyListeners(oldSession, newSession);\n        sessionReady.signalAll();\n    }\n\n    private void notifyListeners(final MetricsSession oldSession, final MetricsSession newSession) {\n        for (final MetricsSessionListener listener : listeners) {\n            try {\n                listener.onSessionChanged(oldSession, newSession);\n            } catch (final Exception e) {\n                log.warn(\"Metrics session listener threw exception\", e);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Represents an authenticated metrics session with a token, shard\n     * assignment, and expiry timestamp.\n     */\n    public static class MetricsSession {\n        public final String token;\n        public final int shardId;\n        public final long expiryMs;\n\n        public MetricsSession(final String token, final int shardId, final long expiryMs) {\n            this.token = token;\n            this.shardId = shardId;\n            this.expiryMs = expiryMs;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public String toString() {\n            return \"MetricsSession{token='\" + token + \"', shard=\" + shardId + \", expiry=\" + expiryMs + \"}\";\n        }\n    }\n}\n","numLines":158,"startLine":1,"totalLines":158}}}

All public methods\n    27→ * are synchronized on this instance's intrinsic monitor. Cache entries\n    28→ * are evicted when they exceed the configured TTL, or when explicitly\n    29→ * invalidated (e.g. after a session shard change during rebalancing).\n    30→ */\n    31→public class TopologyMetricsCache {\n    32→\n    33→    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TopologyMetricsCache.class);\n    34→\n    35→    private final Map<String, CachedMetricsSnapshot> cache = new HashMap<>();\n    36→    private final StreamsMetricsConnector metricsConnector;\n    37→    private final long cacheTtlMs;\n    38→\n    39→    public TopologyMetricsCache(final StreamsMetricsConnector metricsConnector, final long cacheTtlMs) {\n    40→        this.metricsConnector = metricsConnector;\n    41→        this.cacheTtlMs = cacheTtlMs;\n    42→    }\n    43→\n    44→    /**\n    45→     * Returns a cached metrics snapshot for the given topology, refreshing\n    46→     * from the backend if the cache entry is missing or stale.\n    47→     * Returns null if the topology is unknown.\n    48→     */\n    49→    public synchronized CachedMetricsSnapshot getSnapshot(final String topologyName) {\n    50→        final CachedMetricsSnapshot cached = cache.get(topologyName);\n    51→        if (cached != null && !cached.isExpired(cacheTtlMs)) {\n    52→            return cached;\n    53→        }\n    54→        return refreshFromBackend(topologyName);\n    55→    }\n    56→\n    57→    private CachedMetricsSnapshot refreshFromBackend(final String topologyName) {\n    58→        final Map<String, Double> metrics = metricsConnector.fetchLatestMetrics(topologyName);\n    59→        final CachedMetricsSnapshot snapshot = new CachedMetricsSnapshot(topologyName, metrics, System.currentTimeMillis());\n    60→        cache.put(topologyName, snapshot);\n    61→        return snapshot;\n    62→    }\n    63→\n    64→    /**\n    65→     * Invalidates all cached entries. Called when the metrics session's shard\n    66→     * assignment changes, since metrics may now come from a different shard.\n    67→     */\n    68→    public synchronized void invalidateAll() {\n    69→        log.debug(\"Invalidating all {} cached topology metrics snapshots\", cache.size());\n    70→        cache.clear();\n    71→    }\n    72→\n    73→    /**\n    74→     * Invalidates a single topology's cached entry.\n    75→     */\n    76→    public synchronized void invalidateTopology(final String topologyName) {\n    77→        cache.remove(topologyName);\n    78→    }\n    79→\n    80→    /**\n    81→     * @return the number of currently cached snapshots\n    82→     */\n    83→    public synchronized int size() {\n    84→        return cache.size();\n    85→    }\n    86→\n    87→    /**\n    88→     * Creates a {@link MetricsSessionListener} that invalidates this cache\n    89→     * when the session's shard assignment changes. All public methods\n * are synchronized on this instance's intrinsic monitor. Cache entries\n * are evicted when they exceed the configured TTL, or when explicitly\n * invalidated (e.g. after a session shard change during rebalancing).\n */\npublic class TopologyMetricsCache {\n\n    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TopologyMetricsCache.class);\n\n    private final Map<String, CachedMetricsSnapshot> cache = new HashMap<>();\n    private final StreamsMetricsConnector metricsConnector;\n    private final long cacheTtlMs;\n\n    public TopologyMetricsCache(final StreamsMetricsConnector metricsConnector, final long cacheTtlMs) {\n        this.metricsConnector = metricsConnector;\n        this.cacheTtlMs = cacheTtlMs;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns a cached metrics snapshot for the given topology, refreshing\n     * from the backend if the cache entry is missing or stale.\n     * Returns null if the topology is unknown.\n     */\n    public synchronized CachedMetricsSnapshot getSnapshot(final String topologyName) {\n        final CachedMetricsSnapshot cached = cache.get(topologyName);\n        if (cached != null && !cached.isExpired(cacheTtlMs)) {\n            return cached;\n        }\n        return refreshFromBackend(topologyName);\n    }\n\n    private CachedMetricsSnapshot refreshFromBackend(final String topologyName) {\n        final Map<String, Double> metrics = metricsConnector.fetchLatestMetrics(topologyName);\n        final CachedMetricsSnapshot snapshot = new CachedMetricsSnapshot(topologyName, metrics, System.currentTimeMillis());\n        cache.put(topologyName, snapshot);\n        return snapshot;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Invalidates all cached entries. topologyName() {\n            return topologyName;\n        }\n\n        public Map<String, Double> metrics() {\n            return metrics;\n        }\n\n        public long fetchedAtMs() {\n In `renewSessionInternal()` (line 105-125 of MetricsSessionManager.java), `notifyListeners` is called at line 123 while `sessionLock` is held (because `renewSession()` at line 96-102 and `refreshSessionIfExpired()` at line 81-91 both hold `sessionLock` when they call `renewSessionInternal()`). Moving the notification outside the lock would break the cycle.\n\nActually, thinking more carefully about which cycle to break:\n1. We could avoid calling `validateSession` under `transportLock` in `StreamsMetricsConnector`\n\nOption 1 seems cleanest — the session state is already updated before notifying, so moving the notification outside the lock preserves the semantics.\n\nBut there's a subtlety: `renewSessionInternal` is private and called from both `refreshSessionIfExpired` and `renewSession`, both holding `sessionLock`.
